	dynamic $death, 'As in any other city, in Eternal Rome it is reckless to forget to repay money you have borrowed. You died a disgraceful death at the hand of the moneylender''s henchmen...'
end

if contract['active'] = 2: contract['active'] = 0

 gladi_count -= 1
 else
 gladi_count = 10
END

 ride_count -= 1
 else

 $trace[1] = 'ride_start'
 i = 1
 :loop_trace

 $trace[i] = $trace_type[a]

 $trace[12] = 'ride_finish' 
END

!independent slave actions
!added check for health and unconsciousness, if health is zero or it she lying unconscious, the slave will not be able to escape or attack - the_vm
slave_attack = 0
slave_escape = 0
slave_suicide = 0
IF slave["mood"] < 0 and slave['temper'] > slave['obedience']:
 n = 7 + master_cha
 if assistant_state = 1:
  n += assistant["intellect"] + assistant["moral"]
  if assistant_supervise_rule = 1: n += assistant["ego"] + assistant["gladiatrix"]
 end
 chance = RAND(1,n)
 slave_power = slave["gladiatrix"] + slave["stamina"]
 master_power = master_str + master_fighter
 IF chance = 1 and slave['stamina'] > 0 and slave_state = CONST_INT['slave_exist']:
  IF slave['angst'] > 0 and master_power < slave_power:
   slave_attack = 1
   else
   slave_escape = 1
  END
 END 
END

  spawn_milked = 1
  tentacle_hp += 1
  spawn_semen += semen_gain[tentacle_size]
 END 
END

!lactation
slave['milk_gain'] = 0
IF slave['lactation'] > 0:
 slave['milk_gain'] = slave["boobs"] + slave["stamina"] - 3 + slave['mood'] - slave['angst']
 if slave['age'] = CONST_INT['milf_age']: slave['milk_gain'] += 2
 if slave['fat'] = 0: slave['milk_gain'] = slave['milk_gain']/2
 if slave['fat'] > 1: slave['milk_gain'] += 1
 if slave['fat'] > 2: slave['milk_gain'] += 2
 if slave['fat'] > 3: slave['milk_gain'] += 4
 if slave['fat'] > 4: slave['milk_gain'] += 6  
 if slave['fat'] > 5: slave['milk_gain'] += 7  
 if slave['fat'] > 6: slave['milk_gain'] += 8 
 if slave['fat'] > 7: slave['milk_gain'] += 9
 if slave['fat'] > 8: slave['milk_gain'] += 10 
 if slave['fat'] > 9: slave['milk_gain'] += 11
 if slave['fat'] > 10: slave['milk_gain'] +=12
 slave['cream_gain'] = slave['milk_gain']/3
 slave_rate['custom'] += 1
 slave['lactation'] = 1
 if slave['milk_gain'] > 2: slave['lactation'] = 2
 if slave['milk_gain'] > 5: slave['lactation'] = 3
 if slave['milk_gain'] > 8: slave['lactation'] = 4
 if slave['milk_gain'] > 11: slave['lactation'] = 5  
END

!calories counting
slave["calories"] -= 1
food_need = 1
if slave["age"] ! CONST_INT['loli_age']: slave["calories"] -= 1 & food_need += 1
if slave['pregnant'] > 0: slave["calories"] -= 1 & food_need += 1
if slave['egging'] > 0: slave["calories"] -= 2 & food_need += 1
if slave["lactation"] > 0: slave["calories"] -= 1 & food_need += 1
if slave["parasite"] > 0: slave["calories"] -= slave["parasite"]

cal_burn = 0
IF slave["calories"] > 0 and slave_rate["fat"] => 1:
 rise_cap = 5 - slave["stamina"]
 food_health_rise = min (rise_cap, slave["calories"], slave["metabolism"])
 slave_rate["stamina"] += food_health_rise
 slave['starvation'] -= slave['calories']
 slave["calories"] -= slave["metabolism"]
 if slave["calories"] < 0: slave["calories"] = 0
 cal_burn = 1
END

if slave["calories"] = 0: slave['starvation'] -= 1
!removed getting hungry moodlet if the calories are equal to zero
if slave["calories"] < 0: slave['neg_hungry'] = 1 

IF slave["calories"] > 0:
 slave_rate["fat"] += slave["calories"]
 IF slave['starvation'] > 0:
  slave_rate["stamina"] -= slave['calories']
  if  cal_burn = 0: slave['starvation'] -= slave['calories']
 END
 slave["calories"] = 0
END

IF slave["calories"] < 0 and slave["fat"] > 0:
 slave_rate["fat"] -= slave["metabolism"]
 slave["calories"] += slave["metabolism"]
 if slave["calories"] > 0: slave["calories"] = 0
END

IF slave["calories"] < 0:
 if slave["calories"] < -3: slave["calories"] = -3
 slave['starvation'] -= slave["calories"]
 slave['neg_hungry'] = slave['starvation']
END
slave["calories"] = 0

 if slave_4['age'] = CONST_INT['milf_age']: slave_4['milk_gain'] += 2
 if slave_4['fat'] = 0: slave_4['milk_gain'] = slave_4['milk_gain']/2

 if slave_4['fat'] > 3: slave_4['milk_gain'] += 4
 if slave_4['fat'] > 4: slave_4['milk_gain'] += 8

 if slave_4['milk_gain'] > 5: slave_4['lactation'] = 3

 if slave_4['milk_gain'] > 11: slave_4['lactation'] = 5

 eaten_food_3 = food_need_3 + slave_3["stamina"] + slave_3["metabolism"] + 2
 if slave_3["passion_sweets"] > 0: eaten_food_3 += 2
 if slave_3['mood'] < 0: eaten_food_3 -= slave_3['mood'] + slave_3['angst']
 if slave_food_type_3 ! 2: slave_rate_3['custom'] -= 1
END
IF slave_ration_3 = 100: slave_3["pos_cookie"] = 2

if slave_food_type_3 = 0: slave_food_cost_3 = eaten_food_3

IF slave_food_type_3 = 2: 
 IF spawn_semen > eaten_food_3:
  spawn_semen -= eaten_food_3
  else
  slave_food_cost_3 += eaten_food_3 - spawn_semen
  spawn_semen = 0
 END
END

 food_cost_3 += 1

 slave['koffed'] = 0
 a = slave['stamina']*10
 if slave['koffe_addiction'] > a: slave['energy'] -= 1 & slave['neg_slave_koffe'] = 1
 slave['koffe_addiction'] += 1
END
IF slave['on_alco'] > 0:
 slave['on_alco'] = 0
 slave['dipsomania'] += 1
 slave['pos_slave_alco'] = 0
 slave['neg_slave_alco'] = slave['dipsomania']
 else
 if slave['dipsomania'] > 0: slave['dipsomania'] -= 1
END
if slave['dipsomania'] => slave['stamina']: slave_rate['stamina'] -= slave['dipsomania']

 slave['on_meth'] = 0
 if slave['meth_addiction'] > slave['stamina']: slave['neg_slave_meth'] = slave['meth_addiction']
 slave['meth_addiction'] += 1
 slave_rate['stamina'] -= 1
 else
 a = RAND(1,3)
 if a = 1 and slave['meth_addiction'] > 0: slave['meth_addiction'] -= 1
 slave_rate['stamina'] -= slave['meth_addiction']
END

 slave_rate['stamina'] -= slave['opium_addiction']

 slave_rate["wounds"] -= slave["stamina"] + slave["mood"] + slave_healing - slave["hygiene"]

 slave['neg_sick'] = 1
END

 if slave['ill'] > 6: slave['neg_slave_ill'] = slave['ill']

 IF slave["age"] ! CONST_INT['loli_age'] and slave_state ! CONST_INT['no_slave']:
  slave['ovulation'] -= 1

  END
  if slave['cycle_day'] = 9: slave['ovulation'] = 7

 slave['pregnant'] += 1 
 slave_rate['stamina'] -= 1

 IF slave['eggs_to_lay'] = 0:

 END

 else
 slave_rate["angst"] -= slave["mood"] * slave["angst"]
END

 moral_basis = (slave["custom"] + slave["rational"] + slave["instinct"])/3
 moral_boost = min (slave["mood"], moral_basis)
 slave_rate["moral"] += moral_boost
END

END

!Menstrual cycle and pregnancy
IF slave_2["age"] = CONST_INT['loli_age']: slave_2['fertility'] = -2
if slave_2['fertility'] < 0: slave_2['parasite'] = 0
if slave_2['fertility'] < 0: slave_2['pregnant'] = 0
slave_2['cycle_day'] += 1
if slave_2['cycle_day'] > 28: slave_2['cycle_day'] = 1
IF slave_2['pregnant'] = 0: 
 IF slave_2["age"] ! CONST_INT['loli_age'] and slave_state ! CONST_INT['no_slave']:
  slave_2['ovulation'] -= 1
  IF slave_2['cycle_day'] = 1:
   slave_2['neg_menstruation'] = 6 - slave_2['stamina']
   menstruation_2 = 1
  END
  if slave_2['cycle_day'] = 9: slave_2['ovulation'] = 7
 END
 ELSE
 slave_2['pregnant'] += 1 
 slave_rate_2['stamina'] -= 1 
END

IF slave_2['pregnant'] > 3 and slave_2['fertility'] = 1:
 IF slave_2['eggs_to_lay'] = 0:
  virginity_2 = 3
  a = RAND (3,6)
  slave_2['eggs_to_lay'] = slave_2["age"] + slave_2["stamina"] + a + slave_2['fat']
 END
 if slave_2['eggs_to_lay'] = 1: slave_2['pregnant'] = 0
 slave_2['eggs_to_lay'] -= 1
 slave_2['egg_time'] = 1
 slave_rate_2['custom'] += 1  
 if virginity_2 < 2: virginity_2 = 2  
END

!Reduce the mood because of the fear
IF slave_2["fear"] > slave_2["custom"] and slave_2["fear"] > slave_2["ego"] and slave_2["fear"] > slave_2["pride"] :
 if slave_2["fear"] > slave_2["ego"]: slave_2["neg_fear"] = 1
END

!Obtain/reduce Angst
IF slave_2["mood"] < 0:
 angst_rise = 6 - slave_2["sensitivity"] + slave_2["mood"]
 if angst_rise < 0: slave_rate_2["angst"] -= angst_rise
 else
 slave_rate_2["angst"] -= slave_2["mood"] * slave_2["angst"]
END

!growing moral
moral_app = min (slave_2["moral"], slave_2["custom"], slave_2["rational"], slave_2["instinct"])
IF slave_2["angst"] <= 0 and slave_2["mood"] > 0 and moral_app = slave_2["moral"]:
 moral_basis = (slave_2["custom"] + slave_2["rational"] + slave_2["instinct"])/3
 moral_boost = min (slave_2["mood"], moral_basis)
 slave_rate_2["moral"] += moral_boost
END
if slave_2["moral"] > slave_2["fear"] and slave_2["fear"] > 0: slave_2["fear"] -= 1

!lowering spoil
slave_rate_2["spoil"] -= 1 + slave_2["fear"] + slave_2["moral"]

!brand effect
IF slave_2['brand'] > 0: slave_rate_2["custom"] += 1
IF slave_2['brand'] = 1: slave_rate_2["custom"] += 1
IF slave_2['brand'] = 3: slave_rate_2["custom"] += 1

!Forgotten sins and merits
IF slave_2["virtue"] > 0:
 slave_rate_2["mood"] -= slave_2["virtue"]
 if slave_2["virtue"] > slave_2["neg_no_prise"]: slave_2["neg_no_prise"] = slave_2["virtue"]
 slave_2["virtue"] = 0
END

IF slave_2["sin"] > 0:
 if slave_2["sin"] > slave_2["fear"]: slave_2["fear"] -= 1
 if slave_2["fear"] < 0: slave_2["fear"] = 0
 slave_rate_2["fear"] -= slave_2["sin"]
 slave_rate_2["mood"] += slave_2["sin"]
 IF slave_2["spoil"] > 0:
  slave_rate_2["spoil"] += slave_2["sin"]
  else
  if slave_2["pos_no_punish"] < slave_2["sin"] and slave_2["fear"] > 0: slave_2["pos_no_punish"] = slave_2["sin"]  
 END
 slave_2["sin"] = 0
END


!counting the arousal and mood
slave_rate_2["mood"] += slave_2["moral"] + (slave_2["stamina"] - 3) + slave_2["energy"] + daily_bonus["mood"] - slave_2["arousal"] - slave_2["fear"] - slave_2["spoil"] - slave_2["angst"] - slave_2["hygiene"] - (house_mess - 1) - slave_2["mood"]

if slave_2['moral'] > 0: slave_2['pos_moral'] = slave_2['moral']
if slave_2['angst'] > 0: slave_2['neg_angst'] = slave_2['angst']
if slave_2["spoil"] > 0 and slave_2["spoil"] > slave_2["mood"]: slave_2["neg_spoil"] = 1

arousal_modifier = 0
if slave_2["nymphomania"] > 0: arousal_modifier += slave_2["temper"] + slave_2["sensitivity"] + slave_2["mood"]
if slave_2["nymphomania"] < 0: arousal_modifier -= slave_2["temper"] + slave_2["sensitivity"] + slave_2["mood"]
if slave_2["nymphomania"] > -1: slave_rate_2["arousal"] += slave_2["moral"]
slave_rate_2["arousal"] += slave_2["stamina"] + daily_bonus["arousal"] + slave_2["energy"] + slave_2["temper"] + slave_2["mood"] - 6 - slave_2["angst"] + arousal_modifier
slave_2['pos_orgasm'] -= 1 + slave_2["arousal"]
 
a = slave_2['ego'] + slave_2['pride'] + rebell[$slave_psy_basic_2] - slave_2['pos_orgasm']
if slave_2["arousal"] > 0 and a < 0: slave_2['neg_horny'] = 1
if slave_2["nymphomania"] > 1: slave_2['neg_horny'] = 1
if slave_2["nymphomania"] < 0: slave_2['neg_horny'] = 0
!healing and dependence - sub slave_3
IF slave_3['koffed'] > 0:
 slave_3['koffed'] = 0
 a = slave_3['stamina']*10
 if slave_3['koffe_addiction'] > a: slave_3['energy'] -= 1 & slave_3['neg_slave_koffe'] = 1
 slave_3['koffe_addiction'] += 1
END
IF slave_3['on_alco'] > 0:
 slave_3['on_alco'] = 0
 slave_3['dipsomania'] += 1
 slave_3['pos_slave_alco'] = 0
 slave_3['neg_slave_alco'] = slave_3['dipsomania']
 else
 if slave_3['dipsomania'] > 0: slave_3['dipsomania'] -= 1
END
if slave_3['dipsomania'] => slave_3['stamina']: slave_rate_3['stamina'] -= slave_3['dipsomania']

IF slave_3['on_meth'] > 0:
 slave_3['on_meth'] = 0
 if slave_3['meth_addiction'] > slave_3['stamina']: slave_3['neg_slave_meth'] = slave_3['meth_addiction']
 slave_3['meth_addiction'] += 1
 slave_rate_3['stamina'] -= 1
 else
 a = RAND(1,3)
 if a = 1 and slave_3['meth_addiction'] > 0: slave_3['meth_addiction'] -= 1
 slave_rate_3['stamina'] -= slave_3['meth_addiction']
END

IF slave_3['on_opium'] > 0:
 slave_3['on_opium'] = 0
 slave_3['pos_slave_opium'] = 0
 if slave_3['opium_addiction'] > slave_3['stamina']: slave_3['neg_slave_opium'] = slave_3['opium_addiction']
 slave_3['opium_addiction'] += 1
 slave_rate_3['stamina'] -= 1
 else
 a = RAND(1,3)
 if a = 1 and slave_3['opium_addiction'] > 0: slave_3['opium_addiction'] -= 1
 slave_rate_3['stamina'] -= slave_3['opium_addiction']
END

slave_healing = master_medic + assistant["nurse"]
if slave_healing > 0: slave_rate_3["bruises"] -= slave_3["stamina"] + slave_healing

 slave_rate_3["wounds"] -= slave_3["stamina"] + slave_3["mood"] + slave_healing - slave_3["hygiene"]
 slave_rate_3["scares"] += slave_3["wounds"]
 slave_3['neg_sick'] = 1
END

 slave_3['ill'] += 1
 if slave_3['ill'] > slave_3['stamina']: slave_rate_3['stamina'] -= 1
 if slave_3['ill'] > 6: slave_3['neg_slave_ill'] = slave_3['ill']

if slave_5['cycle_day'] > 28: slave_5['cycle_day'] = 1

  slave_5['ovulation'] -= 1
  IF slave_5['cycle_day'] = 1:
   slave_5['neg_menstruation'] = 6 - slave_5['stamina']
   menstruation_5 = 1
  END
  if slave_5['cycle_day'] = 9: slave_5['ovulation'] = 7
 END

 slave_5['pregnant'] += 1 
 slave_rate_5['stamina'] -= 1 
END

END

 slave_rate_5["moral"] += moral_boost
END
if slave_5["moral"] > slave_5["fear"] and slave_5["fear"] > 0: slave_5["fear"] -= 1

!lowering spoil
slave_rate_5["spoil"] -= 1 + slave_5["fear"] + slave_5["moral"]

IF slave_5['brand'] = 1: slave_rate_5["custom"] += 1
IF slave_5['brand'] = 3: slave_rate_5["custom"] += 1

END

 if slave_5["sin"] > slave_5["fear"]: slave_5["fear"] -= 1
 if slave_5["fear"] < 0: slave_5["fear"] = 0
 slave_rate_5["fear"] -= slave_5["sin"]
 slave_rate_5["mood"] += slave_5["sin"]

  slave_rate_5["spoil"] += slave_5["sin"]
  else
  if slave_5["pos_no_punish"] < slave_5["sin"] and slave_5["fear"] > 0: slave_5["pos_no_punish"] = slave_5["sin"]  
 END
 slave_5["sin"] = 0
END

if slave_5["nymphomania"] < 0: arousal_modifier -= slave_5["temper"] + slave_5["sensitivity"] + slave_5["mood"]

slave_rate_5["arousal"] += slave_5["stamina"] + daily_bonus["arousal"] + slave_5["energy"] + slave_5["temper"] + slave_5["mood"] - 6 - slave_5["angst"] + arousal_modifier
slave_5['pos_orgasm'] -= 1 + slave_5["arousal"]
 
a = slave_5['ego'] + slave_5['pride'] + rebell[$slave_psy_basic_5] - slave_5['pos_orgasm']
if slave_5["arousal"] > 0 and a < 0: slave_5['neg_horny'] = 1

 IF pissuar_rule = 1:
  master_mood_rate += slave["sub_piss"] - 3
  if slave["preversion"] < 1: slave['neg_disgust'] = 1
  if slave["sub_piss"] > 2: master_mood['pos_toilet'] = 1
  slave["sub_piss_xp"] += 1
  slave["preversion_xp"] += 1
  slave_rate["mood"] -= 4 - slave["sub_piss"] - slave["moral"]
  if slave["sub_piss"] < 4 and slave["preversion"] < 1: slave["neg_rules"] = 1
  slave_rate["custom"] += 1 
  if slave["sub_piss"] < 3: slave["sub_piss"] += 1
  if master_supermacy > 0: slave_rate["pride"] -= master_supermacy * slave["pride"]
  if master_supermacy <= 0: slave_rate["pride"] -= slave["pride"]     
  slave_rate["hygiene"] += 15  
  slave_rate['stamina'] -= 1
 END
 IF toilet_rule = 1:
  if slave["preversion"] < 2: slave['neg_disgust'] = 1
  master_mood_rate += slave["sub_kopro"] - 3
  slave["preversion_xp"] += 1  
  if slave["sub_kopro"] > 3: master_mood['pos_toilet'] += 1  
  slave_rate["mood"] -= 5 - slave["sub_kopro"] - slave["moral"]
  if slave["sub_kopro"] < 4 and slave["preversion"] < 2: slave["neg_rules"] = 1  
  slave_rate["custom"] += 1 
  if slave["sub_kopro"] < 3: slave["sub_kopro"] += 1
  if master_supermacy > 0: slave_rate["pride"] -= master_supermacy * slave["pride"] * 2
  if master_supermacy <= 0: slave_rate["pride"] -= slave["pride"] * 2   
  slave_rate["hygiene"] += 40 
  slave_rate['stamina'] -= 6 - slave['stamina']
 END
 IF v_balls_rule = 1:
  slave["sub_vaginal_xp"] += 1
  slave_rate["arousal"] += 3
  slave_rate["sensitivity"] += 1
  slave_rate["pride"] -= 1 
  slave_rate["hygiene"] += 5 
 END

rules_broken_3 = iif(rules_res_3 < 0, 1, 0)

IF rules_broken_3 = 1:
 sin_gained_3 = max (1, slave_3["obedience"])
 IF sin_gained_3 > 5: sin_gained_3 = 5
 IF sin_gained_3 => slave_3["virtue"]:
  slave_3["virtue"] = 0
  if sin_gained_3 > slave_3["sin"]: slave_3["sin"] = sin_gained_3
  if sententia_veritas = 1: slave_3["sin"] = 5
 END 
 
 IF silence_rule_3 = 1:
  slave_rate_3["expression"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["temper"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["ego"] += 1  
  slave_rate_3["custom"] -= 1
 END
 IF master_rule_3 = 1:
  slave_rate_3["pride"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["ego"] += 1  
  slave_rate_3["custom"] -= 1 
  slave_rate_3["instinct"] -= slave_3["temper"]
  slave_rate_3["rational"] -= slave_3["ego"]  
 END
 IF shit_prohibited_3 = 1:
  slave_rate_3["ego"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["custom"] -= 1   
 END
 IF pet_rule_3 = 1:
  slave_rate_3["pride"] += 1 
  slave_rate_3["ego"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["custom"] -= 1    
 END
 IF blowjob_rule_3 = 1:
  slave_rate_3["pride"] += 1 
  slave_rate_3["ego"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["custom"] -= 1   
 END
 IF pissuar_rule_3 = 1:
  slave_rate_3["pride"] += 1 
  slave_rate_3["ego"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["custom"] -= 1    
 END
 IF toilet_rule_3 = 1:
  slave_rate_3["pride"] += 1 
  slave_rate_3["ego"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["custom"] -= 1    
 END
 IF v_balls_rule_3 = 1:
  slave_rate_3["pride"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["ego"] += 1  
  slave_rate_3["custom"] -= 1
 END

 ELSE
 IF silence_rule_3 = 1:
  slave_rate_3["callisthenics"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["custom"] += 1  
  slave_rate_3["sensitivity"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["temper"] -= 1
  slave_rate_3["pride"] -= 1
  else
  if slave_3["expression"] < master_artdirector: slave_rate_3["expression"] += 1
 END
 IF master_rule_3 = 1:
  IF master_supermacy > 0:
   slave_rate_3["instinct"] += master_supermacy
   slave_rate_3["rational"] += master_supermacy
   else
   slave_rate_3["instinct"] += 1
   slave_rate_3["rational"] += 1
  END
  slave_rate_3["pride"] -= 1
  slave_rate_3["custom"] += 1
  else
  if slave_3['pride'] > slave_3['moral'] and slave_3['pride'] < slave_3['ego']: slave_rate_3["pride"] += slave_3['pride']
  slave_rate_3["mood"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["instinct"] -= slave_3["temper"]
  slave_rate_3["rational"] -= slave_3["ego"]   
 END
 IF shit_prohibited_3 = 1:
  slave_rate_3["stamina"] -= 1
  slave_rate_3["custom"] += 2
  if master_supermacy > 0: slave_rate_3["pride"] -= master_supermacy
  if master_supermacy <= 0: slave_rate_3["pride"] -= 1  
 END
 IF pet_rule_3 = 1:
  slave_rate_3["custom"] += 1 
  slave_rate_3["ego"] -= 1
  slave_rate_3["callisthenics"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["pet"] += 2
  slave_rate_3["dressage"] += 1
  if master_supermacy > 0: slave_rate_3["pride"] -= master_supermacy
  if master_supermacy <= 0: slave_rate_3["pride"] -= 1   
  slave_rate_3["hygiene"] += 10  
  if slave_3["pet"] => brand_reputation AND slave_3["pet"] > 0: master_mood['pos_good_pet'] = 1
 END
 IF blowjob_rule_3 = 1:
  if master_excitement > 0: master_mood_rate += slave_3["sub_bj"]
  if slave_3["sub_bj"] > 1 and master_excitement > 0: master_mood['pos_good_morning'] = 1
  master_excitement -= 1
  slave_3["sub_bj_xp"] += 1
  slave_concentration += 1
  slave_rate_3["custom"] += 1 
  slave_rate_3["pride"] -= 1 
  slave_rate_3["hygiene"] += 5  
 END
 IF pissuar_rule_3 = 1:
  master_mood_rate += slave_3["sub_piss"] - 3
  if slave_3["preversion"] < 1: slave_3['neg_disgust'] = 1
  if slave_3["sub_piss"] > 2: master_mood['pos_toilet'] = 1
  slave_3["sub_piss_xp"] += 1
  slave_3["preversion_xp"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["mood"] -= 4 - slave_3["sub_piss"] - slave_3["moral"]
  if slave_3["sub_piss"] < 4 and slave_3["preversion"] < 1: slave_3["neg_rules"] = 1
  slave_rate_3["custom"] += 1 
  if slave_3["sub_piss"] < 3: slave_3["sub_piss"] += 1
  if master_supermacy > 0: slave_rate_3["pride"] -= master_supermacy * slave_3["pride"]
  if master_supermacy <= 0: slave_rate_3["pride"] -= slave_3["pride"]     
  slave_rate_3["hygiene"] += 15  
  slave_rate_3['stamina'] -= 1
 END
 IF toilet_rule_3 = 1:
  if slave_3["preversion"] < 2: slave_3['neg_disgust'] = 1
  master_mood_rate += slave_3["sub_kopro"] - 3
  slave_3["preversion_xp"] += 1  
  if slave_3["sub_kopro"] > 3: master_mood['pos_toilet'] += 1  
  slave_rate_3["mood"] -= 5 - slave_3["sub_kopro"] - slave_3["moral"]
  if slave_3["sub_kopro"] < 4 and slave_3["preversion"] < 2: slave_3["neg_rules"] = 1  
  slave_rate_3["custom"] += 1 
  if slave_3["sub_kopro"] < 3: slave_3["sub_kopro"] += 1
  if master_supermacy > 0: slave_rate_3["pride"] -= master_supermacy * slave_3["pride"] * 2
  if master_supermacy <= 0: slave_rate_3["pride"] -= slave_3["pride"] * 2   
  slave_rate_3["hygiene"] += 40 
  slave_rate_3['stamina'] -= 6 - slave_3['stamina']
 END
 IF v_balls_rule_3 = 1:
  slave_3["sub_vaginal_xp"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["arousal"] += 3
  slave_rate_3["sensitivity"] += 1
  slave_rate_3["pride"] -= 1 
  slave_rate_3["hygiene"] += 5 
 END

 pissuar_rule_5_res = 0 
END
IF toilet_rule_5 = 1:
 toilet_rule_5_res = slave_5["obedience"] + slave_5["sub_kopro"] - slave_5["pride"] - slave_5["ego"] - 6 - slave_5["preversion"]
 IF force_rules_5 = 1 and inventory['toilet_stable'] = 1: 
  if toilet_rule_5_res < 0: slave_5['neg_rules'] = 1     
  toilet_rule_5_res = 0
  slave_rate_5["mood"] -= 6 + slave_5["ego"] + slave_5["pride"] - slave_5["moral"] - slave_5["sub_kopro"]
 END
 else
 toilet_rule_5_res = 0
END
!v_balls_rule_5 = 1 - added effect for this rule
IF v_balls_rule_5 = 1:
 v_balls_rule_5_res = slave_5["obedience"] + slave_5["sub_vaginal"] - slave_5["pride"]*2 - slave_5["ego"] - 4
 IF force_rules_5 = 1 and assistant_state = 1:
  if v_balls_rule_5_res < 0: slave_5['neg_rules'] = 1
  v_balls_rule_5_res = 0
  slave_rate_5["mood"] -= 4 + slave_5["pride"] + slave_5["ego"] - slave_5["moral"] - slave_5["sub_vaginal"]
 END
 else
 v_balls_rule_5_res = 0
END

rules_res_5 = min (silence_rule_5_res, master_rule_5_res, shit_prohibited_5_res, pet_rule_5_res, blowjob_rule_5_res, pissuar_rule_5_res, toilet_rule_5_res, v_balls_rule_5_res)
rules_broken_5 = iif(rules_res_5 < 0, 1, 0)

IF rules_broken_5 = 1:
 sin_gained_5 = max (1, slave_5["obedience"])
 IF sin_gained_5 > 5: sin_gained_5 = 5
 IF sin_gained_5 => slave_5["virtue"]:
  slave_5["virtue"] = 0
  if sin_gained_5 > slave_5["sin"]: slave_5["sin"] = sin_gained_5
  if sententia_veritas = 1: slave_5["sin"] = 5
 END 
 
 IF silence_rule_5 = 1:
  slave_rate_5["expression"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["temper"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["ego"] += 1  
  slave_rate_5["custom"] -= 1
 END
 IF master_rule_5 = 1:
  slave_rate_5["pride"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["ego"] += 1  
  slave_rate_5["custom"] -= 1 
  slave_rate_5["instinct"] -= slave_5["temper"]
  slave_rate_5["rational"] -= slave_5["ego"]  
 END
 IF shit_prohibited_5 = 1:
  slave_rate_5["ego"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["custom"] -= 1   
 END
 IF pet_rule_5 = 1:
  slave_rate_5["pride"] += 1 
  slave_rate_5["ego"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["custom"] -= 1    
 END
 IF blowjob_rule_5 = 1:
  slave_rate_5["pride"] += 1 
  slave_rate_5["ego"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["custom"] -= 1   
 END
 IF pissuar_rule_5 = 1:
  slave_rate_5["pride"] += 1 
  slave_rate_5["ego"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["custom"] -= 1    
 END
 IF toilet_rule_5 = 1:
  slave_rate_5["pride"] += 1 
  slave_rate_5["ego"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["custom"] -= 1    
 END
 IF v_balls_rule_5 = 1:
  slave_rate_5["pride"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["ego"] += 1  
  slave_rate_5["custom"] -= 1
 END

 ELSE
 IF silence_rule_5 = 1:
  slave_rate_5["callisthenics"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["custom"] += 1  
  slave_rate_5["sensitivity"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["temper"] -= 1
  slave_rate_5["pride"] -= 1
  else
  if slave_5["expression"] < master_artdirector: slave_rate_5["expression"] += 1
 END
 IF master_rule_5 = 1:
  IF master_supermacy > 0:
   slave_rate_5["instinct"] += master_supermacy
   slave_rate_5["rational"] += master_supermacy
   else
   slave_rate_5["instinct"] += 1
   slave_rate_5["rational"] += 1
  END
  slave_rate_5["pride"] -= 1
  slave_rate_5["custom"] += 1
  else
  if slave_5['pride'] > slave_5['moral'] and slave_5['pride'] < slave_5['ego']: slave_rate_5["pride"] += slave_5['pride']
  slave_rate_5["mood"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["instinct"] -= slave_5["temper"]
  slave_rate_5["rational"] -= slave_5["ego"]   
 END
 IF shit_prohibited_5 = 1:
  slave_rate_5["stamina"] -= 1
  slave_rate_5["custom"] += 2
  if master_supermacy > 0: slave_rate_5["pride"] -= master_supermacy
  if master_supermacy <= 0: slave_rate_5["pride"] -= 1  
 END
 IF pet_rule_5 = 1:
  slave_rate_5["custom"] += 1 
  slave_rate_5["ego"] -= 1
  slave_rate_5["callisthenics"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["pet"] += 2
  slave_rate_5["dressage"] += 1
  if master_supermacy > 0: slave_rate_5["pride"] -= master_supermacy
  if master_supermacy <= 0: slave_rate_5["pride"] -= 1   
  slave_rate_5["hygiene"] += 10  
  if slave_5["pet"] => brand_reputation AND slave_5["pet"] > 0: master_mood['pos_good_pet'] = 1
 END
 IF blowjob_rule_5 = 1:
  if master_excitement > 0: master_mood_rate += slave_5["sub_bj"]
  if slave_5["sub_bj"] > 1 and master_excitement > 0: master_mood['pos_good_morning'] = 1
  master_excitement -= 1
  slave_5["sub_bj_xp"] += 1
  slave_concentration += 1
  slave_rate_5["custom"] += 1 
  slave_rate_5["pride"] -= 1 
  slave_rate_5["hygiene"] += 5  
 END
 IF pissuar_rule_5 = 1:
  master_mood_rate += slave_5["sub_piss"] - 3
  if slave_5["preversion"] < 1: slave_5['neg_disgust'] = 1
  if slave_5["sub_piss"] > 2: master_mood['pos_toilet'] = 1
  slave_5["sub_piss_xp"] += 1
  slave_5["preversion_xp"] += 1

  if slave_5["sub_piss"] < 4 and slave_5["preversion"] < 1: slave_5["neg_rules"] = 1
  slave_rate_5["custom"] += 1 
  if slave_5["sub_piss"] < 3: slave_5["sub_piss"] += 1
  if master_supermacy > 0: slave_rate_5["pride"] -= master_supermacy * slave_5["pride"]
  if master_supermacy <= 0: slave_rate_5["pride"] -= slave_5["pride"]     
  slave_rate_5["hygiene"] += 15  
  slave_rate_5['stamina'] -= 1
 END
 IF toilet_rule_5 = 1:

  master_mood_rate += slave_5["sub_kopro"] - 3
  slave_5["preversion_xp"] += 1

  slave_rate_5["custom"] += 1 
  if slave_5["sub_kopro"] < 3: slave_5["sub_kopro"] += 1

  if master_supermacy <= 0: slave_rate_5["pride"] -= slave_5["pride"] * 2   
  slave_rate_5["hygiene"] += 40 
  slave_rate_5['stamina'] -= 6 - slave_5['stamina']
 END
 IF v_balls_rule_5 = 1:
  slave_5["sub_vaginal_xp"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["arousal"] += 3
  slave_rate_5["sensitivity"] += 1
  slave_rate_5["pride"] -= 1 
  slave_rate_5["hygiene"] += 5 
 END

slave_rate["ego"] -= slave["angst"]

if a < 1 and master_medic > slave["wounds"]: a = 1

if slave["energy"] < -15: slave["energy"] = -15

 slave["energy"] = -14

 slave_masturbating_anyway = 0
END
slave["caught_masturbating"] -= 1


IF slave['pregnant'] => 40 and slave['pregnant_revealed'] = 0: slave['pregnant_revealed'] = 1
IF assistant['pregnant'] => 40 and assistant['pregnant_revealed'] = 0: assistant['pregnant_revealed'] = 1
IF prisoner['pregnant'] => 40 and prisoner['pregnant_revealed'] = 0: prisoner['pregnant_revealed'] = 1

!Morning milking
total_milk_gain = slave['milk_gain'] + assistant['milk_gain'] + prisoner['milk_gain']
total_cream_gain = slave['cream_gain'] + assistant['cream_gain'] + prisoner['cream_gain']
milk_summ += total_milk_gain
cream_summ += total_cream_gain
IF total_milk_gain > 0:
 milking_time = 1
END

:milk_loop
IF milk_summ => 5:
 milk_bottle_plus += 1
 milk_summ -= 5
 jump 'milk_loop'
END

:cream_loop
IF cream_summ => 5:
 cream_bottle_plus += 1
 cream_summ -= 5
 jump 'cream_loop'
END

!egg-laying
total_eggs_gain = slave['egg_time'] + assistant['egg_time'] + prisoner['egg_time']
IF total_eggs_gain > 0:
 egg_time = 1
END

spawn_milked = 0
end_of_the_day = 1
if rules_broken = 1: rules_broken_message = 1

!pet tentacle
IF pet_tentacle > 0:
 tentacle_hp -= 1
 if tentacle_size => 4: tentacle_hp -= 2
 IF tentacle_hp => tentacle_grow[tentacle_size]:
  if tentacle_size < 4: tentacle_grow_event = 1  
 END
 IF tentacle_hp <= tentacle_death[tentacle_size]:
  tentacle_death_event = 1
 END 
END

!Barn stuff goes here
!farmhand lesbian xp accumulation
IF barn_cow = 1 AND farmhand["homosexualism"] = 0: farmhand["lesbian_xp"] + 1
IF barn_harpy = 1 AND farmhand["homosexualism"] = 0: farmhand["lesbian_xp"] + 1
IF farmhand["lesbian_xp"] > 10 AND farmhand["homosexualism"] = 0: farmhand["homosexualism"] = 1
!bonus calculation
IF barn_farmhand = 1:
 barn_farmhand_bonus = 120
 IF barn_farmhand["homosexualism"] = -1: barn_farmhand_bonus -= 10
 IF barn_farmhand["homosexualism"] = 1: barn_farmhand_bonus += 20
 IF barn_farmhand["homosexualism"] = 2: barn_farmhand_bonus += 30
 ELSE
 barn_farmhand_bonus = 100
END

!milking the cow
IF barn_cow_1 = 1:
 cow_1['milk_gain'] = cow_1["boobs"] + cow_1["stamina"] - 3
 if cow_1['age'] = CONST_INT['milf_age']: cow_1['milk_gain'] += 2
 if cow_1['fat'] = 0: cow_1['milk_gain'] = cow_1['milk_gain']/2
 if cow_1['fat'] > 1: cow_1['milk_gain'] += 1
 if cow_1['fat'] > 2: cow_1['milk_gain'] += 2
 if cow_1['fat'] > 3: cow_1['milk_gain'] += 4
 if cow_1['fat'] > 4: cow_1['milk_gain'] += 8  
 cow_1['cream_gain'] = cow_1['milk_gain']/3
 !setting lactation rating
 cow_1['lactation'] = 1
 if cow_1['milk_gain'] > 2: cow_1['lactation'] = 2
 if cow_1['milk_gain'] > 5: cow_1['lactation'] = 3
 if cow_1['milk_gain'] > 8: cow_1['lactation'] = 4
 if cow_1['milk_gain'] > 11: cow_1['lactation'] = 5  
 cow_1['milk_gain'] = cow_1['milk_gain']*barn_farmhand_bonus
 cow_1['milk_gain'] = cow_1['milk_gain']/100
 barn_milk = cow_1['milk_gain']
 barn_cream = cow_1['milk_gain']/3
 !check if the cow_1 has recovered from surgery
 IF cow_1['reabilitation'] > 0:
  cow_1['reabilitation'] -= 1
  cow_1['milk_gain'] = 0
  cow_1['lactation'] = 0
 END 
 !If there is room in the fridge, refill it
 IF frige_space => 5:
  barn_milk += frige["milk"]
  frige["milk"] = 0
  IF barn_milk < 5:
   frige["milk"] = barn_milk
   barn_milk = 0
   ELSE
   frige["milk"] = 5
   barn_milk -= 5
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 5:
  barn_cream += frige["cream"]
  frige["cream"] = 0
  IF barn_cream < 5:
   frige["cream"] = barn_cream
   barn_cream = 0
   ELSE
   frige["cream"] = 5
   barn_cream -= 5
  END
 END
 !Sell any leftover milk and cream - money comes in during end-of-decade billing
 barn_milk_1_profit += barn_milk
 barn_cream_1_profit += barn_cream
 !gradual breast growth
 IF barn_farmhand = 1:
  IF cow_1['reabilitation'] = 0:
   cow_1['days_milked'] += 1
   IF cow_1['days_milked'] = 20:
    cow_1['days_milked'] = 0
    cow_1["boobs"] += 1
    IF cow_1["boobs"] > 8: cow_1["boobs"] = 8
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_G': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_H' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_G' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EE': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_E': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EE' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_E' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BB': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_A': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_HP' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP' 
    if $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DP': $cow_1["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP'

   cow_5['days_milked'] += 1
   IF cow_5['days_milked'] = 20:
    cow_5['days_milked'] = 0
    cow_5["boobs"] += 1
    IF cow_5["boobs"] > 8: cow_5["boobs"] = 8
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_G': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_H' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_G' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EE': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_E': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EE' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_E' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BB': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_A': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_HP' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DP': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CP': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DP' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BP': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CP' 
    if $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_AP': $cow_5["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BP' 
   END
  END
 END
END
IF barn_cow_6 = 1:
 cow_6['milk_gain'] = cow_6["boobs"] + cow_6["stamina"] - 3
 if cow_6['age'] = CONST_INT['milf_age']: cow_6['milk_gain'] += 2
 if cow_6['fat'] = 0: cow_6['milk_gain'] = cow_6['milk_gain']/2
 if cow_6['fat'] > 1: cow_6['milk_gain'] += 1
 if cow_6['fat'] > 2: cow_6['milk_gain'] += 2
 if cow_6['fat'] > 3: cow_6['milk_gain'] += 4
 if cow_6['fat'] > 4: cow_6['milk_gain'] += 8  
 cow_6['cream_gain'] = cow_6['milk_gain']/3
 !setting lactation rating
 cow_6['lactation'] = 1
 if cow_6['milk_gain'] > 2: cow_6['lactation'] = 2
 if cow_6['milk_gain'] > 5: cow_6['lactation'] = 3
 if cow_6['milk_gain'] > 8: cow_6['lactation'] = 4
 if cow_6['milk_gain'] > 11: cow_6['lactation'] = 5  
 cow_6['milk_gain'] = cow_6['milk_gain']*barn_farmhand_bonus
 cow_6['milk_gain'] = cow_6['milk_gain']/100
 barn_milk = cow_6['milk_gain']
 barn_cream = cow_6['milk_gain']/3
 !check if the cow_6 has recovered from surgery
 IF cow_6['reabilitation'] > 0:
  cow_6['reabilitation'] -= 1
  cow_6['milk_gain'] = 0
  cow_6['lactation'] = 0
 END 
 !If there is room in the fridge, refill it
 IF frige_space => 5:
  barn_milk += frige["milk"]
  frige["milk"] = 0
  IF barn_milk < 5:
   frige["milk"] = barn_milk
   barn_milk = 0
   ELSE
   frige["milk"] = 5
   barn_milk -= 5
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 5:
  barn_cream += frige["cream"]
  frige["cream"] = 0
  IF barn_cream < 5:
   frige["cream"] = barn_cream
   barn_cream = 0
   ELSE
   frige["cream"] = 5
   barn_cream -= 5
  END
 END
 !Sell any leftover milk and cream - money comes in during end-of-decade billing
 barn_milk_6_profit += barn_milk
 barn_cream_6_profit += barn_cream
 !gradual breast growth
 IF barn_farmhand = 1:
  IF cow_6['reabilitation'] = 0:
   cow_6['days_milked'] += 1
   IF cow_6['days_milked'] = 20:
    cow_6['days_milked'] = 0
    cow_6["boobs"] += 1
    IF cow_6["boobs"] > 8: cow_6["boobs"] = 8
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_G': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_H' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_G' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EE': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_E': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EE' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_E' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BB': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_A': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_HP' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DP': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP' 
    if $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CP': $cow_6["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DP'

    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EE' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_E' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BB': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_A': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_HP' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DP': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CP': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DP' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BP': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CP' 
    if $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_AP': $cow_10["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BP' 
   END
  END
 END
END
IF barn_cow_11 = 1:
 cow_11['milk_gain'] = cow_11["boobs"] + cow_11["stamina"] - 3
 if cow_11['age'] = CONST_INT['milf_age']: cow_11['milk_gain'] += 2
 if cow_11['fat'] = 0: cow_11['milk_gain'] = cow_11['milk_gain']/2
 if cow_11['fat'] > 1: cow_11['milk_gain'] += 1
 if cow_11['fat'] > 2: cow_11['milk_gain'] += 2
 if cow_11['fat'] > 3: cow_11['milk_gain'] += 4
 if cow_11['fat'] > 4: cow_11['milk_gain'] += 8  
 cow_11['cream_gain'] = cow_11['milk_gain']/3
 !setting lactation rating
 cow_11['lactation'] = 1
 if cow_11['milk_gain'] > 2: cow_11['lactation'] = 2
 if cow_11['milk_gain'] > 5: cow_11['lactation'] = 3
 if cow_11['milk_gain'] > 8: cow_11['lactation'] = 4
 if cow_11['milk_gain'] > 11: cow_11['lactation'] = 5  
 cow_11['milk_gain'] = cow_11['milk_gain']*barn_farmhand_bonus
 cow_11['milk_gain'] = cow_11['milk_gain']/100
 barn_milk = cow_11['milk_gain']
 barn_cream = cow_11['milk_gain']/3
 !check if the cow_11 has recovered from surgery
 IF cow_11['reabilitation'] > 0:
  cow_11['reabilitation'] -= 1
  cow_11['milk_gain'] = 0
  cow_11['lactation'] = 0
 END 
 !If there is room in the fridge, refill it
 IF frige_space => 5:
  barn_milk += frige["milk"]
  frige["milk"] = 0
  IF barn_milk < 5:
   frige["milk"] = barn_milk
   barn_milk = 0
   ELSE
   frige["milk"] = 5
   barn_milk -= 5
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 5:
  barn_cream += frige["cream"]
  frige["cream"] = 0
  IF barn_cream < 5:
   frige["cream"] = barn_cream
   barn_cream = 0
   ELSE
   frige["cream"] = 5
   barn_cream -= 5
  END
 END
 !Sell any leftover milk and cream - money comes in during end-of-decade billing
 barn_milk_11_profit += barn_milk
 barn_cream_11_profit += barn_cream
 !gradual breast growth
 IF barn_farmhand = 1:
  IF cow_11['reabilitation'] = 0:
   cow_11['days_milked'] += 1
   IF cow_11['days_milked'] = 20:
    cow_11['days_milked'] = 0
    cow_11["boobs"] += 1
    IF cow_11["boobs"] > 8: cow_11["boobs"] = 8
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_G': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_H' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_G' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EE': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_E': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_F' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EE' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_E' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DD' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_D' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BB': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CC' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_C' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_A': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_B' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_HP' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_FP' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DP': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_EP' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CP': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_DP' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BP': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_CP' 
    if $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_AP': $cow_11["boobs_img"] = 'boobs_BP' 
   END
  END
 END

!eggs.
IF barn_harpy_1 = 1:
 !calculate egg amount
 a = RAND (3,6)
 barn_harpy_1_eggs = harpy_1["age"] + harpy_1["stamina"] + a + harpy_1['fat']
 harpy_1['egglaying'] = 1
 !set egglaying rating
 if barn_harpy_1_eggs > 5: harpy_1['egglaying'] = 2
 if barn_harpy_1_eggs > 7: harpy_1['egglaying'] = 3
 if barn_harpy_1_eggs > 9: harpy_1['egglaying'] = 4
 if barn_harpy_1_eggs > 12: harpy_1['egglaying'] = 5
 barn_harpy_1_eggs = barn_harpy_1_eggs*barn_farmhand_bonus
 barn_harpy_1_eggs = barn_harpy_1_eggs/100
 !check to see if harpy_1''s recovered from surgery
 IF harpy_1['reabilitation'] > 0:
  harpy_1['reabilitation'] -= 1
  barn_harpy_1_eggs = 0
  harpy_1['egglaying'] = 0
 END 
 !refill the fridge 
 IF frige_space => 5:
  barn_harpy_1_eggs += frige["eggs"]
  frige["eggs"] = 0
  IF barn_harpy_1_eggs < 5:
   frige["eggs"] = barn_harpy_1_eggs
   barn_harpy_1_eggs = 0
   ELSE
   frige["eggs"] = 5
   barn_harpy_1_eggs -= 5
  END
 END
 !sell any leftover eggs
 barn_egg_1_profit += barn_harpy_1_eggs
END

   frige["eggs"] = 5
   barn_harpy_9_eggs -= 5
  END
 END
 !sell any leftover eggs
 barn_egg_9_profit += barn_harpy_9_eggs
END
!eggs.
IF barn_harpy_10 = 1:
 !calculate egg amount
 a = RAND (3,6)
 barn_harpy_10_eggs = harpy_10["age"] + harpy_10["stamina"] + a + harpy_10['fat']
 harpy_10['egglaying'] = 1
 !set egglaying rating
 if barn_harpy_10_eggs > 5: harpy_10['egglaying'] = 2
 if barn_harpy_10_eggs > 7: harpy_10['egglaying'] = 3
 if barn_harpy_10_eggs > 9: harpy_10['egglaying'] = 4
 if barn_harpy_10_eggs > 12: harpy_10['egglaying'] = 5
 barn_harpy_10_eggs = barn_harpy_10_eggs*barn_farmhand_bonus
 barn_harpy_10_eggs = barn_harpy_10_eggs/100
 !check to see if harpy_10''s recovered from surgery
 IF harpy_10['reabilitation'] > 0:
  harpy_10['reabilitation'] -= 1
  barn_harpy_10_eggs = 0
  harpy_10['egglaying'] = 0
 END 
 !refill the fridge 
 IF frige_space => 5:
  barn_harpy_10_eggs += frige["eggs"]
  frige["eggs"] = 0
  IF barn_harpy_10_eggs < 5:
   frige["eggs"] = barn_harpy_10_eggs
   barn_harpy_10_eggs = 0
   ELSE
   frige["eggs"] = 5
   barn_harpy_10_eggs -= 5
  END
 END
 !sell any leftover eggs
 barn_egg_10_profit += barn_harpy_10_eggs
END

!cow_1 food calc and weight gain

 barn_cow_1_food += 2 + cow_1['lactation'] + cow_1['age']
 IF barn_farmhand_fattens = 1 AND barn_farmhand = 1:
  barn_cow_1_food += 5
  cow_1_rate['fat'] += 5
 END
 IF cow_1['fat'] = 0:
  if cow_1_rate['fat'] => 10: cow_1['fat'] = 1 & cow_1_rate['fat'] = 0 
 END
 IF cow_1['fat'] = 1:
  if cow_1_rate['fat'] => 10: cow_1['fat'] = 2 & cow_1_rate['fat'] = 0

  if cow_1_rate['fat'] => 20: cow_1['fat'] = 3 & cow_1_rate['fat'] = 0

  if cow_1_rate['fat'] => 40: cow_1['fat'] = 4 & cow_1_rate['fat'] = 0 
 END
 IF cow_1['fat'] = 4:
  if cow_1_rate['fat'] => 60: cow_1['fat'] = 5 & cow_1_rate['fat'] = 0 
 END
 IF cow_1['fat'] = 5:
  if cow_1_rate['fat'] => 80: cow_1['fat'] = 6 & cow_1_rate['fat'] = 0 
 END
 IF cow_1['fat'] = 6:
  if cow_1_rate['fat'] => 120: cow_1['fat'] = 7 & cow_1_rate['fat'] = 0 
 END
 IF cow_1['fat'] = 7:
  if cow_1_rate['fat'] => 140: cow_1['fat'] = 8 & cow_1_rate['fat'] = 0 
 END
 IF cow_1['fat'] = 8:
  if cow_1_rate['fat'] => 160: cow_1['fat'] = 9 & cow_1_rate['fat'] = 0 
 END
 IF cow_1['fat'] = 9:
  if cow_1_rate['fat'] => 180: cow_1['fat'] = 10 & cow_1_rate['fat'] = 0

 IF harpy_12['stamina'] < 3: harpy_12_rate['stamina'] += 2
 IF harpy_12['stamina'] = 0:
  if harpy_12_rate['stamina'] => 10: harpy_12['stamina'] = 1 & harpy_12_rate['stamina'] = 0 
 END
 IF harpy_12['stamina'] = 1:
  if harpy_12_rate['stamina'] => 10: harpy_12['stamina'] = 2 & harpy_12_rate['stamina'] = 0 
 END
 IF harpy_12['stamina'] = 2:
  if harpy_12_rate['stamina'] => 20: harpy_12['stamina'] = 3 & harpy_12_rate['stamina'] = 0 
 END
 IF harpy_12['stamina'] = 4:
  if harpy_12_rate['stamina'] <= -80: harpy_12['stamina'] = 3 & harpy_12_rate['stamina'] = 0
 END
 IF harpy_12['stamina'] = 5:
  if harpy_12_rate['stamina'] <= -80: harpy_12['stamina'] = 4 & harpy_12_rate['stamina'] = 0  
 END
 IF harpy_12['stamina'] = 6:
  if harpy_12_rate['stamina'] <= -80: harpy_12['stamina'] = 5 & harpy_12_rate['stamina'] = 0  
 END
 IF harpy_12['stamina'] = 7:
  if harpy_12_rate['stamina'] <= -80: harpy_12['stamina'] = 6 & harpy_12_rate['stamina'] = 0  
 END
 IF harpy_12['stamina'] = 8:
  if harpy_12_rate['stamina'] <= -80: harpy_12['stamina'] = 7 & harpy_12_rate['stamina'] = 0  
 END
 IF harpy_12['stamina'] = 9:
  if harpy_12_rate['stamina'] <= -80: harpy_12['stamina'] = 8 & harpy_12_rate['stamina'] = 0  
 END
 IF harpy_12['stamina'] = 10:
  if harpy_12_rate['stamina'] <= -80: harpy_12['stamina'] = 9 & harpy_12_rate['stamina'] = 0  
 END
END

!pig_1 slaughter
IF barn_pig_1 = 1 AND pig_1['fat'] = 10 AND barn_farmhand = 1 AND barn_farmhand_slaughters = 1:
 !adapted from the regular sell-for-meat code
 base_meat_gain = (pig_1["boobs"] + 2)
 if pig_1["fat"] > 0: base_meat_gain = base_meat_gain*2
 mince_gain = 0
 mince_bonus = 0
 if pig_1["fat"] = 1: mince_gain = pig_1["boobs"]
 if pig_1["fat"] = 2: mince_gain = pig_1["boobs"]*2
 if pig_1["fat"] = 3: mince_gain = pig_1["boobs"]*3
 if pig_1["fat"] = 4: mince_gain = pig_1["boobs"]*4
 if pig_1["fat"] = 5: mince_gain = pig_1["boobs"]*5
 if pig_1["fat"] = 6: mince_gain = pig_1["boobs"]*5
 if pig_1["fat"] = 7: mince_gain = pig_1["boobs"]*5
 if pig_1["fat"] = 8: mince_gain = pig_1["boobs"]*5
 if pig_1["fat"] = 9: mince_gain = pig_1["boobs"]*5
 if pig_1["fat"] = 10: mince_gain = pig_1["boobs"]*5
 if mince_gain < pig_1["fat"]: mince_gain = pig_1["fat"] 
 meat_max = 1 + pig_1["stamina"]
 IF base_meat_gain > meat_max:
  meat_gain = meat_max
  mince_bonus = base_meat_gain - meat_max
  else
  meat_gain = base_meat_gain
 END
 mince_gain += mince_bonus
 IF pig_1['age'] = CONST_INT['loli_age']:
  virgin_meat_gain = meat_gain
  meat_gain = 0
 END
 IF pig_1['age'] = CONST_INT['young_age'] and virginity = 0:
  virgin_meat_gain = meat_gain
  meat_gain = 0
 END
 !kill the pig_1
 barn_pig_1 = 0
 pig_1_state = CONST_INT['no_slave']
 killvar 'pig_1' 
 killvar '$pig_1'
 killvar 'pig_1_rate' 
 killvar 'already_done_pig_1'
 killvar 'pig_1_inventory'
 prise_promised_pig_1 = 0
 gift_promised_pig_1 = 0
 prise_promised_pig_1 = 0
 abandon_treat_pig_1 = 0
 death_treat_pig_1 = 0
 pig_1_slave_sleep_condition = 0
 pig_1_slave_food_type = 0
 pig_1_slave_eats_remains = 0
 pig_1_slave_ration = 0
 pig_1_slave_food_portion = 0
 pig_1_vitamin = 0
 pig_1_silence_rule = 0
 pig_1_master_rule = 0
 pig_1_orgasm_prohibited = 0
 pig_1_shit_prohibited = 0
 pig_1_pet_rule = 0
 pig_1_blowjob_rule = 0
 pig_1_pissuar_rule = 0
 pig_1_toilet_rule = 0
 pig_1_slave_cleans_rule = 0
 pig_1_slave_cooks_rule = 0
 pig_1_slave_washes_rule = 0
 pig_1_slave_tentacle_rule = 0
 pig_1_v_balls_rule = 0
 pig_1_rule_masturbation = 0
 !refill the fridge
 IF frige_space => 5 AND estate_size[$estate] = 50:
  mince_gain += frige["mince"]
  frige["mince"] = 0
  IF mince_gain < 5:
   frige["mince"] = mince_gain
   mince_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["mince"] = 5
   mince_gain -= 5
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 5 AND estate_size[$estate] = 50:
  meat_gain += frige["meat"]
  frige["meat"] = 0
  IF meat_gain < 5:
   frige["meat"] = meat_gain
   meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["meat"] = 5
   meat_gain -= 5
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 5 AND estate_size[$estate] = 50:
  virgin_meat_gain += frige["virgin_meat"]
  frige["virgin_meat"] = 0
  IF virgin_meat_gain < 5:
   frige["virgin_meat"] = virgin_meat_gain
   virgin_meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["virgin_meat"] = 5
   virgin_meat_gain -= 5
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 10 AND estate_size[$estate] = 100:
  mince_gain += frige["mince"]
  frige["mince"] = 0
  IF mince_gain < 10:
   frige["mince"] = mince_gain
   mince_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["mince"] = 10
   mince_gain -= 10
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 10 AND estate_size[$estate] = 100:
  meat_gain += frige["meat"]
  frige["meat"] = 0
  IF meat_gain < 10:
   frige["meat"] = meat_gain
   meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["meat"] = 10
   meat_gain -= 10
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 10 AND estate_size[$estate] = 100:
  virgin_meat_gain += frige["virgin_meat"]
  frige["virgin_meat"] = 0
  IF virgin_meat_gain < 10:
   frige["virgin_meat"] = virgin_meat_gain
   virgin_meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["virgin_meat"] = 10
   virgin_meat_gain -= 10
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 15 AND estate_size[$estate] = 150:
  mince_gain += frige["mince"]
  frige["mince"] = 0
  IF mince_gain < 15:
   frige["mince"] = mince_gain
   mince_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["mince"] = 15
   mince_gain -= 15
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 15 AND estate_size[$estate] = 150:
  meat_gain += frige["meat"]
  frige["meat"] = 0
  IF meat_gain < 15:
   frige["meat"] = meat_gain
   meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["meat"] = 15
   meat_gain -= 15
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 15 AND estate_size[$estate] = 150:
  virgin_meat_gain += frige["virgin_meat"]
  frige["virgin_meat"] = 0
  IF virgin_meat_gain < 15:
   frige["virgin_meat"] = virgin_meat_gain
   virgin_meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["virgin_meat"] = 15
   virgin_meat_gain -= 15
  END
 END 
 barn_pig_1_profit += mince_gain*20 + meat_gain*20 + virgin_meat_gain*20
END

!pig_5 slaughter
IF barn_pig_5 = 1 AND pig_5['fat'] = 10 AND barn_farmhand = 1 AND barn_farmhand_slaughters = 1:
 !adapted from the regular sell-for-meat code
 base_meat_gain = (pig_5["boobs"] + 2)
 if pig_5["fat"] > 0: base_meat_gain = base_meat_gain*2
 mince_gain = 0
 mince_bonus = 0
 if pig_5["fat"] = 1: mince_gain = pig_5["boobs"]
 if pig_5["fat"] = 2: mince_gain = pig_5["boobs"]*2
 if pig_5["fat"] = 3: mince_gain = pig_5["boobs"]*3
 if pig_5["fat"] = 4: mince_gain = pig_5["boobs"]*4
 if pig_5["fat"] = 5: mince_gain = pig_5["boobs"]*5
 if pig_5["fat"] = 6: mince_gain = pig_5["boobs"]*5
 if pig_5["fat"] = 7: mince_gain = pig_5["boobs"]*5
 if pig_5["fat"] = 8: mince_gain = pig_5["boobs"]*5
 if pig_5["fat"] = 9: mince_gain = pig_5["boobs"]*5
 if pig_5["fat"] = 10: mince_gain = pig_5["boobs"]*5
 if mince_gain < pig_5["fat"]: mince_gain = pig_5["fat"] 
 meat_max = 1 + pig_5["stamina"]
 IF base_meat_gain > meat_max:
  meat_gain = meat_max
  mince_bonus = base_meat_gain - meat_max
  else
  meat_gain = base_meat_gain
 END
 mince_gain += mince_bonus
 IF pig_5['age'] = CONST_INT['loli_age']:
  virgin_meat_gain = meat_gain
  meat_gain = 0
 END
 IF pig_5['age'] = CONST_INT['young_age'] and virginity = 0:
  virgin_meat_gain = meat_gain
  meat_gain = 0
 END

 IF frige_space => 5 AND estate_size[$estate] = 50:
  mince_gain += frige["mince"]
  frige["mince"] = 0
  IF mince_gain < 5:
   frige["mince"] = mince_gain
   mince_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["mince"] = 5
   mince_gain -= 5
  END
 END

   meat_gain = 0

   virgin_meat_gain -= 5

 END

!pig_9 slaughter
IF barn_pig_9 = 1 AND pig_9['fat'] = 10 AND barn_farmhand = 1 AND barn_farmhand_slaughters = 1:
 !adapted from the regular sell-for-meat code
 base_meat_gain = (pig_9["boobs"] + 2)
 if pig_9["fat"] > 0: base_meat_gain = base_meat_gain*2
 mince_gain = 0
 mince_bonus = 0
 if pig_9["fat"] = 1: mince_gain = pig_9["boobs"]
 if pig_9["fat"] = 2: mince_gain = pig_9["boobs"]*2
 if pig_9["fat"] = 3: mince_gain = pig_9["boobs"]*3
 if pig_9["fat"] = 4: mince_gain = pig_9["boobs"]*4
 if pig_9["fat"] = 5: mince_gain = pig_9["boobs"]*5
 if pig_9["fat"] = 6: mince_gain = pig_9["boobs"]*5
 if pig_9["fat"] = 7: mince_gain = pig_9["boobs"]*5
 if pig_9["fat"] = 8: mince_gain = pig_9["boobs"]*5
 if pig_9["fat"] = 9: mince_gain = pig_9["boobs"]*5
 if pig_9["fat"] = 10: mince_gain = pig_9["boobs"]*5
 if mince_gain < pig_9["fat"]: mince_gain = pig_9["fat"] 
 meat_max = 1 + pig_9["stamina"]
 IF base_meat_gain > meat_max:
  meat_gain = meat_max
  mince_bonus = base_meat_gain - meat_max
  else
  meat_gain = base_meat_gain
 END
 mince_gain += mince_bonus
 IF pig_9['age'] = CONST_INT['loli_age']:
  virgin_meat_gain = meat_gain
  meat_gain = 0
 END
 IF pig_9['age'] = CONST_INT['young_age'] and virginity = 0:
  virgin_meat_gain = meat_gain
  meat_gain = 0
 END

 if pig_12["fat"] = 10: mince_gain = pig_12["boobs"]*5
 if mince_gain < pig_12["fat"]: mince_gain = pig_12["fat"] 
 meat_max = 1 + pig_12["stamina"]
 IF base_meat_gain > meat_max:
  meat_gain = meat_max
  mince_bonus = base_meat_gain - meat_max
  else
  meat_gain = base_meat_gain
 END
 mince_gain += mince_bonus
 IF pig_12['age'] = CONST_INT['loli_age']:
  virgin_meat_gain = meat_gain
  meat_gain = 0
 END
 IF pig_12['age'] = CONST_INT['young_age'] and virginity = 0:
  virgin_meat_gain = meat_gain
  meat_gain = 0
 END
 !kill the pig_12
 barn_pig_12 = 0
 pig_12_state = CONST_INT['no_slave']
 killvar 'pig_12' 
 killvar '$pig_12'
 killvar 'pig_12_rate' 
 killvar 'already_done_pig_12'
 killvar 'pig_12_inventory'
 prise_promised_pig_12 = 0
 gift_promised_pig_12 = 0
 prise_promised_pig_12 = 0
 abandon_treat_pig_12 = 0
 death_treat_pig_12 = 0
 pig_12_slave_sleep_condition = 0
 pig_12_slave_food_type = 0
 pig_12_slave_eats_remains = 0
 pig_12_slave_ration = 0
 pig_12_slave_food_portion = 0
 pig_12_vitamin = 0
 pig_12_silence_rule = 0
 pig_12_master_rule = 0
 pig_12_orgasm_prohibited = 0
 pig_12_shit_prohibited = 0
 pig_12_pet_rule = 0
 pig_12_blowjob_rule = 0
 pig_12_pissuar_rule = 0
 pig_12_toilet_rule = 0
 pig_12_slave_cleans_rule = 0
 pig_12_slave_cooks_rule = 0
 pig_12_slave_washes_rule = 0
 pig_12_slave_tentacle_rule = 0
 pig_12_v_balls_rule = 0
 pig_12_rule_masturbation = 0
 !refill the fridge
 IF frige_space => 5 AND estate_size[$estate] = 50:
  mince_gain += frige["mince"]
  frige["mince"] = 0
  IF mince_gain < 5:
   frige["mince"] = mince_gain
   mince_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["mince"] = 5
   mince_gain -= 5
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 5 AND estate_size[$estate] = 50:
  meat_gain += frige["meat"]
  frige["meat"] = 0
  IF meat_gain < 5:
   frige["meat"] = meat_gain
   meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["meat"] = 5
   meat_gain -= 5
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 5 AND estate_size[$estate] = 50:
  virgin_meat_gain += frige["virgin_meat"]
  frige["virgin_meat"] = 0
  IF virgin_meat_gain < 5:
   frige["virgin_meat"] = virgin_meat_gain
   virgin_meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["virgin_meat"] = 5
   virgin_meat_gain -= 5
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 10 AND estate_size[$estate] = 100:
  mince_gain += frige["mince"]
  frige["mince"] = 0
  IF mince_gain < 10:
   frige["mince"] = mince_gain
   mince_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["mince"] = 10
   mince_gain -= 10
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 10 AND estate_size[$estate] = 100:
  meat_gain += frige["meat"]
  frige["meat"] = 0
  IF meat_gain < 10:
   frige["meat"] = meat_gain
   meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["meat"] = 10
   meat_gain -= 10
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 10 AND estate_size[$estate] = 100:
  virgin_meat_gain += frige["virgin_meat"]
  frige["virgin_meat"] = 0
  IF virgin_meat_gain < 10:
   frige["virgin_meat"] = virgin_meat_gain
   virgin_meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["virgin_meat"] = 10
   virgin_meat_gain -= 10
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 15 AND estate_size[$estate] = 150:
  mince_gain += frige["mince"]
  frige["mince"] = 0
  IF mince_gain < 15:
   frige["mince"] = mince_gain
   mince_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["mince"] = 15
   mince_gain -= 15
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 15 AND estate_size[$estate] = 150:
  meat_gain += frige["meat"]
  frige["meat"] = 0
  IF meat_gain < 15:
   frige["meat"] = meat_gain
   meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["meat"] = 15
   meat_gain -= 15
  END
 END
 IF frige_space => 15 AND estate_size[$estate] = 150:
  virgin_meat_gain += frige["virgin_meat"]
  frige["virgin_meat"] = 0
  IF virgin_meat_gain < 15:
   frige["virgin_meat"] = virgin_meat_gain
   virgin_meat_gain = 0
   ELSE
   frige["virgin_meat"] = 15
   virgin_meat_gain -= 15
  END
 END 
 barn_pig_12_profit += mince_gain*20 + meat_gain*20 + virgin_meat_gain*20
END

GT 'end_day_screen'
